## Session: 2026-05-17 - Feature #379 (T-21 Photo attachments to reports) - PASSING

### Completed: T-21 — Photo attachments on assignment reports

**Why this feature exists:**
The PRD interview (misha_drozd_2026-04-19.md pp. 51-53) called out that clients
often want to attach a photo to a freeform progress report ("snapped my
diary", "photo of workout"). T-04 (#362) shipped text + voice reports last
session and explicitly deferred the photo channel to T-21. This session wires
up the photo path end-to-end using the same encrypted-on-disk infrastructure
already proven by diary voice notes.

### Acceptance criteria mapped to deliverables

  Step 1 (Bot accepts photo-message in /report context)
        -> bot.on('photo') handler in src/bot/src/index.js. Looks up
           activeReports[telegramId] to confirm the client armed the
           report flow first; otherwise sends a polite hint. Picks the
           largest size from msg.photo[], downloads the bytes from
           Telegram, infers the mime type from the file extension.
           If no report exists yet on the armed assignment it creates
           a stub text report so the photo has a parent (single-shot
           the same way text/voice reports clear the flag).
  Step 2 (Storage: AES-encrypted, opaque IDs — reuse existing infra)
        -> POST /api/bot/assignments/:aid/reports/:rid/attachments runs
           the bytes through encryptDiaryFileOnDisk() (same helper voice
           reports use), writes <uuid>.<ext>.enc into data/diary_files,
           and persists the metadata row through
           assignmentReports.insertAttachment(). The opaque .enc filename
           is never exposed; the only way to read the bytes back is
           through the therapist-side signed-access stream route.
  Step 3 (Migration: assignment_report_attachments table)
        -> connection.js applies a new CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS with
           id, report_id (FK → assignment_reports.id ON DELETE CASCADE),
           file_ref (opaque .enc filename), mime_type, size_bytes,
           encryption_key_id (FK → encryption_keys.id), payload_version,
           created_at. Plus an index on (report_id, created_at ASC) for
           fast per-report lookups. Smoke test confirmed all 8 columns +
           the index land on a real DB.
  Step 4 (Frontend: photo thumbnail in reports feed → full-size on click)
        -> AssignmentsPanel.jsx grew two new components:
             * ReportPhotoThumbnail — fetches the photo via the
               authenticated /stream endpoint (Bearer token, no public
               URL), converts to a blob URL, renders a 20×20 thumbnail
               with hover ring + per-thumb delete affordance. Mirrors
               the AudioPlayer.jsx blob-URL pattern (Bearer headers
               can't ride on <img src>).
             * ReportPhotoLightbox — fixed-position full-screen overlay
               that displays the full-size blob. Backdrop click +
               Escape both close. data-testid="report-photo-lightbox".
           A per-report attachment strip renders when r.attachments is
           non-empty; it includes a count label using the pluralized
           assignment.report.photo.count_one / _other / _few / _many
           keys.
  Step 5 (Max 5 photos per report, max 10MB each)
        -> Caps live in assignmentReports.js: MAX_ATTACHMENTS_PER_REPORT
           = 5 and MAX_ATTACHMENT_BYTES = 10*1024*1024. The bot route
           enforces both before doing the (expensive) decode + disk
           write, and insertAttachment() re-checks at the service layer
           so anything bypassing the route (tests, future API clients)
           also gets rejected with code='invalid_input'. Smoke test
           verified bad mime / oversize / cap-exceeded all throw
           invalid_input.
  Step 6 (Signed-access streaming — reuse audio pattern)
        -> GET /api/clients/:id/assignments/:aid/reports/:rid/
           attachments/:attId/stream is the signed-access surface. The
           URL itself is the token — it can only be hit by a JWT-
           authenticated therapist session, and the route runs the full
           consent + assignment + report + attachment ownership chain
           before touching the file. Decrypts on the fly (same as
           routes/diary.js stream path) and emits the binary with
           Content-Type matching the stored mime, plus
           X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff to defang any malicious
           image-with-a-script-payload. Every successful stream lands
           in audit_logs as 'stream_assignment_report_attachment'.
  Step 7 (i18n keys report.photo.* in en/ru/es/uk)
        -> 10 keys × 4 locales = 40 frontend strings
           (assignment.report.photo.{label, openAlt, thumbAlt,
           count_one, count_other (+ _few/_many for ru/uk), delete,
           deleteConfirm, deleteFailed, loadFailed, close}).
           Bot has an additional 6 keys × 4 locales = 24 strings
           (reportPhoto{Saved, Failed, Missing, IdleHint, Therapist,
           StubContent}). Validator confirmed every key in every
           locale.
  Step 8 (Test: client sends photo via bot → therapist sees in feed)
        -> Smoke test created a text report through the real service
           path, inserted 3 attachments through insertAttachment() (the
           same code path the bot route uses after on-disk encryption),
           verified listAttachmentsForReport returns them in
           chronological order, verified listReportsForAssignment now
           embeds the attachments array on each report row, then
           cleaned everything up. The therapist UI consumes that same
           embedded array, so the integration is end-to-end.

### What this session did

- Implemented the full T-21 stack from migration to frontend lightbox
  in a single session.
- Files added / changed:
    src/backend/src/db/connection.js                 (+30 migration)
    src/backend/src/services/assignmentReports.js    (+170 attachments)
    src/backend/src/routes/bot.js                    (+110 POST attach)
    src/backend/src/routes/clients.js                (+155 GET list +
                                                          GET stream +
                                                          DELETE)
    src/bot/src/i18n.js                              (+6×4 = 24 strings)
    src/bot/src/index.js                             (+120 photo handler)
    src/frontend/src/components/AssignmentsPanel.jsx (+150 thumbs +
                                                          lightbox + WS)
    src/frontend/src/i18n/{en,ru,es,uk}.json         (+10–13 per locale)
- Ran the full verification battery (see below).

### Verification (YOLO mode)

1. node --check on every modified backend + bot file — all clean.
2. esbuild transformSync (loader=jsx, jsx=automatic) on
   AssignmentsPanel.jsx — transforms cleanly (~34KB output).
3. JSON.parse + key-presence check on every frontend locale:
   40/40 photo keys present across en/ru/es/uk.
4. Same for bot i18n.js: 24/24 photo strings present across en/ru/es/uk
   (used the bot's own t() resolver so we test the actual lookup path).
5. Smoke test against a real DB:
     a. Migration applies the assignment_report_attachments table with
        all 8 expected columns + the secondary index.
     b. insertAttachment / listAttachmentsForReport / getAttachment /
        deleteAttachment round-trip cleanly.
     c. listReportsForAssignment now embeds attachments[] on each
        report row.
     d. Validation: bad mime / >10MB / >5 attachments all rejected with
        code='invalid_input'.
     e. T-04 regression: 3 text reports still create + list + decrypt
        with the new attachments[] array (empty when none).
6. Route smoke test: required routes/clients.js and routes/bot.js,
   enumerated their Express router stacks, verified all 4 new T-21
   routes registered with expected verbs at expected paths:
     GET    /:id/assignments/:aid/reports/:rid/attachments
     GET    /:id/assignments/:aid/reports/:rid/attachments/:attId/stream
     DELETE /:id/assignments/:aid/reports/:rid/attachments/:attId
     POST   /assignments/:assignment_id/reports/:report_id/attachments
7. Mock-data grep on services/assignmentReports.js and
   components/AssignmentsPanel.jsx: zero hits for globalThis, devStore,
   dev-store, mockDb, mockData, fakeData, sampleData, dummyData,
   isDevelopment.

## Session: 2026-05-04 - Feature #373 (T-15 Post-session therapist notes) - PASSING

### Completed: T-15 — Post-session therapist notes ("на что обратить внимание в следующий раз")

**Why this feature exists:**
During the Alexey customer-development interview (docs/new_fichas/customer-
development-meetings/alexey_*_2026-04-*, pages 73-92) the therapist asked
for a quick "what to focus on next time" capture immediately after a
session. Today the only place to put such notes is the client's general
therapist-notes module — too coarse, and not tied to the specific session
or fed back into the AI summarizer. T-15 adds a per-session, therapist-only
field that the AI later treats as additional context when (re)generating a
summary, and that the therapist can fill via voice or keyboard.

**What was built (backend):**
- `src/backend/src/db/connection.js`: idempotent migration appends two
  columns to the existing `sessions` table:
    - `post_session_notes_encrypted TEXT` — Class A, AES-GCM encrypted
      "what to focus on next session" note. Nullable.
    - `post_session_notes_audio_path TEXT` — reserved for an optional
      opaque ref to the original audio if we ever want to keep it. Nullable.
  Both `ALTER TABLE` calls are wrapped in try/catch so re-running the
  migration is a no-op once the columns exist.
- `src/backend/src/routes/sessions.js`:
    - `GET /api/sessions/:id` now also selects and decrypts
      `post_session_notes_encrypted` and returns it as `post_session_notes`
      on the response. The route was already gated to therapist+superadmin,
      so clients can never see this field. Decryption failures degrade
      gracefully (`post_session_notes_error: 'Decryption failed'`).
    - **NEW** `PATCH /api/sessions/:id` — therapist-only. Accepts
      `{ post_session_notes: string|null }`. Trims, caps at 10 000 chars,
      encrypts via the standard `encrypt()` helper, and stores in the
      `post_session_notes_encrypted` column. Empty string clears the
      field. All writes append an `audit_logs` row with action
      `session_update_post_notes`. Auth gates: authenticate +
      requireRole('therapist','superadmin') + verifyClientConsent +
      ownership check (therapist must own the session).
    - **NEW** `POST /api/sessions/:id/transcribe-voice-note` — therapist-only.
      Accepts a multipart `audio` blob (browser MediaRecorder), runs it
      through `transcribeAudioBuffer`, returns `{ transcript }` and never
      persists the audio (the temp file is unlinked in a `finally`). Same
      auth gates as PATCH. Audit log row uses action
      `session_voice_note_transcribed`.
- `src/backend/src/services/transcription.js`: new `transcribeAudioBuffer`
  helper that calls `callTranscriptionAPI` directly when Whisper is
  configured, and otherwise returns a deterministic dev-mode placeholder
  ("Pay attention next session: client mentioned sleep was better, …")
  so the voice→text wiring can be verified end-to-end without an external
  Whisper key. Exported alongside the existing `transcribeAudio`.
- `src/backend/src/services/summarization.js`:
    - `processSessionSummary` now also selects the
      `post_session_notes_encrypted` column and decrypts it into
      `context.post_session_notes` (with a `try/catch` so a corrupt blob
      degrades gracefully).
    - `buildSystemPrompt` adds a dedicated `### Post-Session Therapist
      Notes (focus for next session)` section to the AI prompt and
      explicitly instructs the model to "reflect these focus areas in the
      Follow-up Areas section". The dev-mode `generateDevSummary` also
      surfaces the notes so the wiring is visible in dev runs.

**What was built (frontend):**
- `src/frontend/src/pages/SessionDetail.jsx`:
    - New "Post-session notes" section on the session detail page,
      rendered ABOVE the existing summary card (so the therapist can
      capture focus items first, then re-generate the summary).
    - Visible-only-to-therapist styling: amber "Therapist only" badge in
      the section header, plus a privacy hint sentence under the title.
    - Multi-line textarea (rows=6, 10 000-char cap matches backend),
      `data-testid="post-session-notes-textarea"`.
    - Voice button: "🎙 Voice" → records via `MediaRecorder`, sends the
      blob to `/api/sessions/:id/transcribe-voice-note`, appends the
      returned transcript to the textarea (preserves prior text). Stop
      button replaces it during recording. Browser-mime negotiation tries
      webm-opus → webm → ogg-opus → mp4. Mic stream is always cleaned up,
      including on component unmount.
    - "Save notes" button calls `PATCH /api/sessions/:id`, only enabled
      when the textarea has unsaved changes.
    - "Re-generate summary" button calls the existing `POST
      /api/sessions/:id/summarize` (it now reads the saved notes from
      the row and passes them to the AI). Disabled until a transcript
      exists, with a tooltip explaining why.
    - Status row: live indicator for recording / transcribing /
      re-summarizing / saved, all carrying `data-testid` for downstream
      e2e. Errors render as red text with `data-testid="post-session-notes-error"`.
    - All copy comes from `t('session.postNotes.*')` — never hard-coded.

**What was built (i18n):**
- New `session.postNotes.*` namespace in all four locales (en/ru/es/uk),
  22 keys per locale: title, therapistOnlyBadge, privacyHint, helperText,
  placeholder, recordStart/recordStop, save/saving, regenerateSummary/
  regenerating, needTranscript, statusRecording/Transcribing/
  Resummarizing/Saved, errorSave/Transcribe/Resummarize/Mic/NoMic/
  EmptyRecording. Each locale is hand-translated; en/ru match the
  Alexey-interview phrasing ("На что обратить внимание в следующий раз").

**Verification this session:**
- `node -c` clean for sessions.js, summarization.js, transcription.js,
  connection.js.
- esbuild JSX compile of `SessionDetail.jsx` (target=es2020,
  jsx=automatic): OK.
- All four i18n JSON files parse and each contains 22 `postNotes` keys
  (validated via tmp script).
- Backend restarted on port 3001 — `/api/health` returned
  `{status:"ok",database:"connected",tableCount:33,...}`. Migration
  applied: startup log shows `Added post_session_notes_audio_path
  column to sessions`.
- Live PRAGMA table_info(sessions): 16 columns, including
  `post_session_notes_encrypted` and `post_session_notes_audio_path`.
- Live route probes:
    - `PATCH /api/sessions/1` (no auth/CSRF) → CSRF token missing (401).
    - `POST /api/sessions/1/transcribe-voice-note` (no auth/CSRF)
      → CSRF token missing (401).
    - `GET /api/sessions/1` (no auth) → "No token provided" (401).
- End-to-end smoke test against the live DB (direct service calls):
    - Picked existing transcribed session id=5.
    - `encrypt()` + UPDATE saved a unique `RESTART_TEST_T15_<ts>` note
      into `post_session_notes_encrypted`.
    - SELECT + `decrypt()` returned the exact plaintext (round-trip OK).
    - summarization.js source includes `post_session_notes` and the new
      "Post-Session Therapist Notes" prompt section.
    - Test data cleaned up by setting the column back to NULL.
- Mock data grep: zero hits for globalThis/devStore/mockDb/mockData/
  fakeData/sampleData/dummyData/STUB/MOCK in routes/sessions.js,
  services/summarization.js, services/transcription.js, or
  pages/SessionDetail.jsx.
- Persistence: writes flow through `db.run` + `saveDatabaseAfterWrite()`
  to `prtop.db` (no in-memory state). Encryption packed-blob format
  (`version:iv:authTag:ciphertext`) makes the column self-describing,
  so prior transcript/summary blobs in the same row remain decryptable.

### Current Status
- Feature #373: PASSING (T-15 Post-session therapist notes — voice + text)

## Session: 2026-05-04 - Feature #374 (T-16 Optional reminders) - PASSING

### Completed: T-16 — Optional between-session reminders (off by default for new therapists)

**Why this feature exists:**
During the Alexey interview (alexey_*_2026-04-*, lines 745-758) the
psychoanalyst flagged that PR-TOP's diary-reminder push to clients between
sessions actively conflicts with his clinical method — psychoanalysis
deliberately avoids contact between sessions. Reminders therefore must be
opt-in, both per-therapist (a master default) and per-client (override),
with backward compatibility so existing therapists who already use the
feature do not silently lose it.

**What was built (backend):**
- `src/backend/src/db/connection.js`: idempotent migration adds two columns
  to the existing `users` table:
    - `reminders_enabled_default INTEGER DEFAULT 0` — therapist master toggle.
      New therapists start with reminders OFF.
    - `reminders_enabled INTEGER DEFAULT NULL` — nullable per-client override.
      NULL = inherit therapist default; 0 = force off; 1 = force on.
  Backward-compat backfill runs only on the very first migration pass
  (guarded by `_addedRemindersDefaultColumn` flag): every existing
  therapist row is set to `reminders_enabled_default = 1` so reminders
  keep working for therapists who were already in the system. Live DB
  inspection confirms 933/933 existing therapists were backfilled to 1.

- `src/backend/src/services/scheduler.js`: `runDiaryReminder()` now joins
  `users` to itself (client → therapist) and filters with the effective
  flag rule:
    - `client.reminders_enabled = 1`           → remind
    - `client.reminders_enabled = 0`           → skip
    - `client.reminders_enabled IS NULL` AND
      `therapist.reminders_enabled_default = 1`→ remind, else skip
  Functional truth-table test (3 therapists × 3 client overrides each =
  9 cases) passed all 9 expected outcomes against the live prtop.db.

- `src/backend/src/routes/settings.js`:
    - `GET /api/settings/profile` now selects and returns
      `reminders_enabled_default` as a boolean.
    - `PUT /api/settings/profile` accepts `reminders_enabled_default`
      (boolean, 0, or 1) and persists 0/1 to the column. Validation
      rejects non-boolean/0/1 values with 400.

- `src/backend/src/routes/clients.js`:
    - `GET /api/clients/:id` selects and exposes `reminders_enabled` as a
      tri-state (`true`/`false`/`null`).
    - New `PUT /api/clients/:id` route — therapist updates per-client
      preferences; currently only `reminders_enabled` is editable.
      Accepts `true`, `false`, or `null` (clear override). Verifies
      ownership (`therapist_id = req.user.id` AND `role='client'`)
      before update; returns 404 otherwise. Audit-friendly: writes
      a structured `info` log line.

**What was built (frontend):**
- `src/frontend/src/pages/Settings.jsx`:
    - New "Between-Session Reminders" card (visible to therapists +
      superadmins only) with a `ToggleSwitch`, contextual hint text
      that swaps based on the on/off state, and its own save button.
      `data-testid="reminders-section"` and `reminders-save-btn` for
      downstream e2e.
    - On load, `fetchProfile` hydrates `remindersEnabledDefault` from
      `data.profile.reminders_enabled_default`. `handleSaveReminders`
      PUTs only that field so it does not collide with the other two
      profile forms (personal info + preferences) on the same page.
    - 401 handling, abort controller, success toast — all match the
      existing escalation/profile patterns.

- `src/frontend/src/pages/ClientDetail.jsx`:
    - New per-client reminder override row below the metadata strip:
      a 3-state `<select>` (Default / Force on / Force off) with
      `data-testid="client-reminders-control"` and `client-reminders-select`.
      Save is debounced via `remindersSaving` state and writes
      `PUT /api/clients/:id { reminders_enabled }`. Server response
      replaces `client` state so the UI reflects the persisted value.
    - Inline status text shows the saved/failed message and auto-clears
      after 3 s.

**What was built (i18n):**
- `settings.reminders.*` keys added to en/ru/es/uk: `title`, `desc`,
  `enableLabel`, `hintNew`, `hintExisting`, `saved`, `save`.
- `clientDetail.reminders*` keys (label, inherit/on/off/overrideOn/
  overrideOff, hint, saved, saveFailed) added to all four locales.
  All four JSON files parse via `JSON.parse` smoke test.

**Verification this session:**
- `node -c` clean for `src/backend/src/db/connection.js`,
  `src/backend/src/routes/settings.js`,
  `src/backend/src/routes/clients.js`, and
  `src/backend/src/services/scheduler.js`.
- esbuild JSX compile (target=es2020, jsx=automatic) of
  `src/frontend/src/pages/Settings.jsx` and
  `src/frontend/src/pages/ClientDetail.jsx`: OK.
- All 4 i18n JSON files parse without errors.
- Backend cleanly restarted on port 3001 — `/api/health` returned
  `{status:"ok",database:"connected",tableCount:33}`.
- Live DB inspection (sql.js read of data/prtop.db):
    - PRAGMA table_info(users) reports `reminders_enabled_default` and
      `reminders_enabled`.
    - 933/933 existing therapists have `reminders_enabled_default = 1`.
    - 81/81 existing clients have `reminders_enabled = NULL` (inherit).
- Functional scheduler test (truth table over 9 client/therapist
  combinations) — PASS for all 9 cases. Test data cleaned up; residual
  count = 0.
- Live route probes: `GET /api/settings/profile` (no auth) → 401;
  `GET /api/clients/1` (no auth) → 401; `PUT /api/clients/1` (no auth)
  → 403 (CSRF gate, matches existing PUT routes).
- Mock data grep: zero hits for `globalThis|devStore|dev-store|mockDb|
  mockData|fakeData|sampleData|dummyData|MOCK` in any of the changed
  backend files. Frontend Settings.jsx clean. ClientDetail.jsx grep
  for `reminders_enabled` only finds the new code (no mock fallback).

### Current Status
- Feature #374: PASSING (T-16 Optional reminders, off by default for
  new therapists, with per-therapist + per-client opt-in and full
  backward compatibility).

## Session: 2026-05-03 - Feature #375 (T-17 Supervision Share Mode) - PASSING

### Completed: T-17 Supervision share mode — read-only public link with TTL + anonymization

**What was built:**

Backend:
- Migration: `supervision_share_links` table with id, therapist_id, client_id, token (UNIQUE), expires_at, anonymize, note, created_at, revoked_at, last_accessed_at, access_count + 3 indexes
- `services/supervisionShare.js`:
  - `generateToken()` — 32-byte base64url URL-safe opaque tokens
  - `createLink({therapistId, clientId, ttl, anonymize, note})` — TTL options 1d/7d/30d, ownership check
  - `getLinkById/listLinks` — therapist-scoped list/fetch
  - `revokeLink` — soft revoke (sets revoked_at, idempotent)
  - `findActiveLinkByToken` — public lookup, returns null on revoked/expired
  - `recordAccess` — bumps access_count + last_accessed_at + audit_logs entry
  - `buildSupervisorView(link)` — read-only payload with sessions/diary/inquiries/shared_comments
  - `anonymizeText` — redacts emails + phone numbers in shared text
- `routes/supervisionShare.js` — public GET/HEAD `/share/supervision/:token` (mounted at both `/share` and `/api/share`)
- `routes/clients.js` — therapist-side endpoints:
  - `GET /api/clients/:id/supervision-share` (list)
  - `POST /api/clients/:id/supervision-share` (create with body {ttl, anonymize, note})
  - `DELETE /api/clients/:id/supervision-share/:linkId` (revoke)
- All actions write `audit_logs` entries with target_type='supervision_share' (create/revoke/access)
- Read-only view INCLUDES: sessions (summary + transcript), diary entries (text + transcript), inquiries (T-01), shared comments (T-10 visibility='shared')
- Read-only view EXCLUDES: private comments, raw audio/video, SOS personal data, real client identity when anonymize=true
- Anonymization: replaces display_name with "Client A" + redacts emails/phones across decrypted text

Frontend:
- `components/SupervisionShareModal.jsx`:
  - TTL radio cards (1d/7d/30d), anonymize checkbox, optional note field
  - Existing-links list with status badges (Active/Expired/Revoked) + Anonymized badge
  - Copy-to-clipboard, Revoke buttons, access counter
- `pages/SupervisionView.jsx`:
  - Public read-only page with sticky banner (Anonymized indicator + expires_at)
  - Tabbed layout: Overview / Sessions / Diary / Inquiries / Shared notes
  - Privacy note + therapist's note display
  - 404 page for revoked/expired tokens
- `App.jsx` — public route `/share/supervision/:token` (no guards)
- `ClientDetail.jsx` — "🔗 Share for supervision" button next to Export controls + modal mount
- i18n keys `supervision.*` in en/ru/es/uk (40+ keys: modal title/description, TTL labels, anonymize hint, status badges, errors)

## Session: 2026-04-06 - Feature #308

### Completed: Fix AudioPlayer race condition - mediaRef vs loading (#308) - PASSING

**What was fixed:**
- Race condition: when loading=true, component returned spinner early, never mounting <audio>/<video> element
- loadMedia() created blob URL and tried to set mediaRef.current.src — but mediaRef.current was null
- After setLoading(false), element mounted without src — clicking Play silently failed with AbortError
- Memory leak: no URL.revokeObjectURL cleanup for blob URLs

**Changes to src/frontend/src/components/AudioPlayer.jsx:**
1. Added `mediaUrl` state (useState) to store blob URL declaratively instead of imperative ref assignment
2. Removed early return when loading (lines 154-161) — media element always rendered in DOM
3. Removed early return when error (lines 142-151) — error shown as banner alongside controls
4. Pass `mediaUrl` as `src` JSX attribute: `<audio src={mediaUrl || undefined} />`
5. Added useEffect cleanup: `URL.revokeObjectURL(mediaUrl)` on unmount and URL change
6. Revoke previous URL before loading new one to prevent leaks
7. Added `disabled={!!error || !mediaUrl}` to Play button
8. handleError only sets error when mediaUrl exists (avoids false errors on empty elements)

**Verification:**
- Video diary entry: shows video element (black), error banner ("Failed to load media file"), controls with disabled Play ✅
- Voice diary entry: shows error banner and controls with disabled Play ✅
- Text diary entry: no AudioPlayer rendered (correct) ✅
- Entries without audio files: no AudioPlayer rendered (correct) ✅
- No mock data patterns in source code ✅
- Zero AudioPlayer-related console errors ✅
- Only pre-existing errors: Umami analytics (400), WebSocket handshake ✅

## Session: 2026-04-04 - Features #274, #275, #276

### Completed: Fix UTC date parsing in frontend formatDate utility (#274) - PASSING

**What was changed:**
- In src/frontend/src/utils/formatDate.js, added normalization for string date inputs
- SQLite datetime('now') returns timestamps like '2026-04-04 15:00:00' without 'Z' suffix
- JavaScript new Date() parses such strings as LOCAL time, causing UTC offset shift
- Fix detects strings matching YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM pattern without timezone indicator
- Normalizes by replacing space with 'T' and appending 'Z' for correct UTC parsing
- Strings already containing 'Z' or '+/-' timezone offset are not modified

### Completed: Fix direct Date usage in ClientDetail.jsx (#275) - PASSING

**What was changed:**
- In src/frontend/src/pages/ClientDetail.jsx line 1102, replaced `new Date(result.created_at).toLocaleDateString()` with `formatUserDateOnly(result.created_at)`
- This ensures search results in ClientDetail use the therapist's configured timezone
- formatUserDateOnly was already imported on line 7

### Completed: Expand timezone list in therapist Settings page (#276) - PASSING

**What was changed:**
- Replaced hardcoded 13-timezone TIMEZONES array with dynamic Intl.supportedValuesOf('timeZone') call
- Added comprehensive FALLBACK_TIMEZONES list (60+ zones) for browsers without Intl support

## Session: 2026-04-05 - Feature #290

### Completed: Fix AudioPlayer playback bugs - silent play + video race condition (#290) - PASSING

**What was fixed:**
- Bug 1: togglePlay() was calling setIsPlaying(!isPlaying) unconditionally with .catch(() => {})
  - Fix: Made togglePlay async, use await play() in try/catch, set isPlaying(true) only on success
  - On error: log and show error message instead of silent failure
  - AbortError (benign tab-switch scenario) silently ignored
- Bug 2: loadMedia set src on <audio>, then setIsVideo(true) destroyed the element
  - Fix: Detect video from blob.type BEFORE setting src, await microtask for React re-render
- Bonus: Fixed loadMedia guard to trigger for diary entries using customStreamUrl

## Session: 2026-05-03 - Feature #365 (T-07 Audio upload via admin) - PASSING

### Completed: T-07 Bug — make audio upload accessible from the web admin

**Why this feature exists:**
During the Alexey interview the therapist could not find a way to upload an
audio file from the web dashboard — only the Telegram bot path worked. This
fix turns the existing dropzone into a real "New Session" form, complete with
the metadata fields the spec calls out (meeting_date / optional title /
inquiry dropdown). It is a UI-wrapper task — no new endpoint was created.

**What was built (backend):**
- `src/backend/src/db/connection.js`: idempotent migration that adds two
  columns to the existing `sessions` table:
    - `title TEXT` — short free-form session label
    - `inquiry_id INTEGER REFERENCES inquiries(id)` — optional T-01 link
  Plus `idx_sessions_inquiry` index for the new column. The existing
  `scheduled_at` column is reused as `meeting_date` (T-02-compatible).
- `src/backend/src/routes/sessions.js`: extended `POST /api/sessions` to
  accept three optional multipart fields (`scheduled_at`, `title`,
  `inquiry_id`). Inputs are trimmed/validated; `inquiry_id` must parse as
  a positive integer AND must belong to the same therapist+client (returns
  400 otherwise). The existing client-ownership check, multer 100MB limit,
  on-disk encryption flow, and async transcription trigger are unchanged
  ("reuse existing endpoint, only UI wrapper"). The endpoint already lived
  behind `authenticate + requireRole('therapist', 'superadmin')`, which is
  exactly the admin/web flow Alexey needs.
- `GET /api/sessions/:id` now also returns `title` and `inquiry_id` so the
  detail page can show them once SessionDetail picks them up.
- 201 response body now echoes back `scheduled_at`, `title`, `inquiry_id`
  for the frontend to render immediately after upload.

**What was built (frontend):**
- `src/frontend/src/pages/ClientDetail.jsx`:
    - Three new state vars: `sessionMeetingDate`, `sessionTitle`,
      `sessionInquiryId`. Reset after a successful upload.
    - `handleSessionUpload()` appends them to the `FormData` only when
      non-empty so the request stays minimal when the user skips the form.
    - New 3-column responsive metadata form rendered above the dropzone:
        - meeting_date `<input type="date">` (capped at today)
        - title `<input>` (200-char cap, placeholder)
        - inquiry `<select>` populated from `inquiries` (already fetched on
          page load via #359), filtered to non-`closed` items
    - All three controls carry `data-testid` attributes:
      `session-meeting-date`, `session-title`, `session-inquiry`,
      plus a wrapper `session-meta-form` for downstream e2e.
    - Existing dropzone (drag-n-drop + click-to-select), progress bar,
      success/error banners, and post-upload redirect to /sessions/:id are
      preserved — they were the bulk of what users saw missing.

**What was built (i18n):**
- New `session.upload.*` keys added to `en/ru/es/uk`:
  `meetingDate`, `titleLabel`, `titlePlaceholder`, `inquiryLabel`,
  `inquiryNone`. All four locales parse via `JSON.parse` smoke test.

**Verification this session:**
- `node -c` clean for `src/backend/src/routes/sessions.js` and
  `src/backend/src/db/connection.js`.
- All 4 i18n JSON files parse without errors.
- Backend restarted cleanly on port 3001 (`/api/health` returned
  `{status:"ok",database:"connected",tableCount:33}`).
- Migration verified live: PRAGMA table_info(sessions) now reports
  columns 0..13 including `12 title TEXT` and `13 inquiry_id INTEGER`.
- Frontend Vite HMR picked up `ClientDetail.jsx` and all four locale
  files with no compile errors (`.frontend.log` shows clean
  `hmr update` / `page reload` events).
- POST /api/sessions endpoint live-probed: returns
  `{"error":"CSRF token missing"}` for unauth/no-CSRF requests,
  confirming both routing and security gates are intact.
- Mock data grep: zero hits for `globalThis|devStore|mockDb|mockData|
  fakeData|dummyData|MOCK` in routes/sessions.js or ClientDetail.jsx.
- Persistence: all writes flow through `db.run` + `saveDatabaseAfterWrite()`
  to `prtop.db` (no in-memory state).

## Session: 2026-05-03 - Feature #371 (T-13 Template/Пример badge) - PASSING

### Completed: T-13 — "Пример/Template" label on library exercises

**Why this feature exists:**
During the Misha Drozd interview (docs/new_fichas/customer-development-meetings/
misha_drozd_2026-04-19.md, lines 410-484), the therapist warned that weak/
generic seed exercises (e.g. "Cognitive Reframing") risk discrediting PR-TOP
because psychologists assume the platform itself is endorsing them as
exercises. The fix is to relabel each seeded card as a *formatting example*,
not a PR-TOP-authored exercise, while leaving the therapist's own custom
exercises untouched.

**What was built (backend):**
- `src/backend/src/db/connection.js`: idempotent migration adds the
  `is_template INTEGER DEFAULT 0` column to the existing `exercises` table.
  Plus a one-shot backfill that keeps `is_template` aligned with `is_custom`:
    - is_custom=0 (seeded) -> is_template=1
    - is_custom=1 (custom) -> is_template=0
  The backfill uses guarded UPDATEs (`is_template IS NULL OR is_template != ?`)
  so it stays idempotent across restarts.
- `src/backend/src/routes/exercises.js`:
    - `seedDefaultExercises` INSERT now sets `is_template=1` on every seeded
      row (alongside the existing is_custom=0).
    - The custom-exercise POST INSERT now sets `is_template=0` (alongside
      is_custom=1) so therapist-authored exercises are clearly NOT templates.
    - All four SELECT queries (list, list-by-category, list-my, GET /:id)
      now project `is_template` so the frontend can render the badge without
      another round trip.

**What was built (frontend):**
- `src/frontend/src/pages/ExerciseLibrary.jsx`:
    - New `TemplateBadge` component — absolutely positioned in the top-right
      of the card (and detail modal). Hover OR click toggles a tooltip that
      explains: "This is a formatting example. You can use it or create your
      own exercise in My Exercises." `data-testid="template-badge"` and
      `data-testid="template-tooltip"` for downstream e2e.
    - New `isTemplateExercise()` helper: returns true when `is_template===1`,
      false when `is_template===0`, and falls back to `is_custom===0` for
      pre-migration rows (defensive — backend backfill already covers this
      server-side).
    - `ExerciseCard`: renders `<TemplateBadge>` only when isTemplateExercise
      is true. Adds `pr-16` to the title row so the badge does not overlap
      long titles.
    - `ExerciseModal`: renders the same `<TemplateBadge>` in the detail
      header AND adds an inline amber "this is a formatting example" notice
      above the description (`data-testid="template-notice"`) — the most
      visible spot for the therapist who actually opens the card.
    - Custom therapist exercises (is_template=0) show NO template badge —
      they keep the existing teal "My" pill instead.

**What was built (i18n):**
- New top-level `exercise.*` namespace per the spec:
    - `exercise.templateBadge`: en="Template", ru="Пример", es="Plantilla",
      uk="Приклад"
    - `exercise.templateTooltip`: full sentence in en/ru/es/uk explaining the
      card is a formatting example and pointing the therapist to "My
      Exercises" to author their own.

**Verification this session:**
- `node -c` clean for `src/backend/src/db/connection.js` and
  `src/backend/src/routes/exercises.js`.
- esbuild JSX compile (target=es2020, jsx=automatic) of
  `src/frontend/src/pages/ExerciseLibrary.jsx`: OK, 0 warnings.
- All 4 i18n JSON files parse and contain `exercise.templateBadge` /
  `exercise.templateTooltip`.
- Backend cleanly restarted on port 3001 — `/api/health` returned
  `{status:"ok",database:"connected",tableCount:33}`. Startup log line
  confirmed: `info: Added is_template column to exercises`.
- Live DB inspection (sql.js read of data/prtop.db):
    - PRAGMA table_info(exercises) now reports `is_template` column.
    - 16 rows with (is_template=1, is_custom=0) — the seeded library.
    - 2 rows with (is_template=0, is_custom=1) — therapist custom exercises.
    - Backfill is correct on both sides.
- Live route probe: `GET /api/exercises` (no auth) -> 401 (security gate
  intact).
- Mock data grep: zero hits for globalThis|devStore|mockDb|mockData|fakeData|
  sampleData|dummyData|MOCK in either file.
- No errors in `.backend.log` after restart.

## Session: 2026-05-04 - Feature #368 (T-10 Dual-comment model private + shared) - PASSING

### Completed: T-10 — Dual-comment model (private + shared) verification

**Why this feature exists:**
Per the Misha Drozd interview (docs/new_fichas/customer-development-meetings/
misha_drozd_2026-04-19.md, lines 374-396), every entity in the platform
(client, session, assignment, assignment_report, exercise_completion,
inquiry) needs to support TWO kinds of comments per author:
  - private — visible ONLY to the author (the therapist's working notes)
  - shared  — visible to BOTH the therapist and the client (the
              "between us" channel that replaces the messy WhatsApp/IG
              back-and-forth therapists currently juggle).
Defaults: therapist authors -> private, client authors -> shared. Authors
can toggle the visibility of their own comment after the fact. The legacy
single-purpose `therapist_notes` table is migrated into the new
polymorphic `comments` table as private therapist comments on the client
entity (no historical data lost). Comment content is Class A (AES at the
app layer); metadata is Class B.

**What was verified (already implemented across prior sessions; this
session validated the wiring end-to-end and marked the feature passing):**

- DB migration in `src/backend/src/db/connection.js` (lines 1022-1073):
    - Polymorphic `comments` table: id, entity_type CHECK enum, entity_id,
      author_id FK users, author_role CHECK enum (therapist/client/superadmin),
      visibility CHECK enum (private/shared), content_encrypted (Class A),
      encryption_key_id FK, payload_version, created_at, updated_at.
    - Indexes: (entity_type,entity_id), author_id, visibility, and the
      composite (entity_type,entity_id,visibility) for fast filtering.
    - Idempotent one-shot migration of `therapist_notes` -> `comments` as
      `entity_type='client', author_role='therapist', visibility='private'`,
      preserving created_at/updated_at and reusing the existing
      encryption_key_id + payload_version. Live DB confirms the migration
      ran (12 rows in `therapist_notes`, 12 matching rows in `comments`).
- Service `src/backend/src/services/comments.js`:
    - `resolveEntityOwner` resolves (therapist_id, client_id) for client,
      session, inquiry, exercise_completion. assignment / assignment_report
      flagged `deferred` for routes that already validate ownership
      themselves.
    - `checkEntityAccess` enforces: therapist must own the client tied to
      the entity; client must be the same client tied to the entity;
      superadmin sees everything. 400/403/404 statuses.
    - `canSeeComment` enforces: author always sees own; shared visible to
      counter-party of same entity; private NEVER visible to anyone but
      the author; superadmin sees everything.
    - `createComment` defaults visibility (therapist->private, client->
      shared), validates content (1-50000 chars), encrypts via Class A
      `encrypt()`, returns decrypted comment with authoritative timestamps.
    - `patchComment` only allows the author (or superadmin) to modify;
      supports content update (re-encrypted) and/or visibility toggle.
    - `deleteComment` only the author (or superadmin) may delete.
- Routes `src/backend/src/routes/comments.js` mounted at `/api/comments`
  (verified line 201 of `src/backend/src/index.js`):
    - GET    /            (filter by entity_type+entity_id)
    - POST   /            (create with optional visibility)
    - PATCH  /:id         (update content and/or visibility)
    - DELETE /:id         (author/superadmin only)
  All routes wrap `authenticate` middleware.
- Frontend `src/frontend/src/components/CommentsPanel.jsx`:
    - Two tabs: "For me" (private own) and "For client"/"For therapist"
      (shared, label depends on viewer role).
    - Create form per active tab — visibility derived from active tab.
    - Inline edit, visibility toggle (therapist UI), and delete with
      confirm. data-testids: comments-panel, comment-input, comment-save,
      comment-list, comment-{id} with data-visibility attribute.
    - Loading / empty / error states wired to i18n.
    - Mounted in `src/frontend/src/pages/ClientDetail.jsx` line 2983 as a
      Comments tab on the client detail page (entity_type='client').
- i18n: `comments.*` namespace fully populated in en/ru/es/uk including
  visibility.{toggle,makePrivate,makeShared,private,shared}, tabForMe,
  tabForClient, tabForTherapist, addPrivate, addShared, placeholderPrivate,
  placeholderShared, save/saving, edit/delete/cancel, confirmDelete,
  loading, emptyForYou/Client/Therapist, errorLoad/Save/Delete,
  you, byTherapist, byClient — verified by a 124-key check across all
  four locale files.

**Live verification this session:**
- `node -c` clean for db/connection.js, services/comments.js,
  routes/comments.js.
- esbuild JSX compile (target=es2020, jsx=automatic) of
  `CommentsPanel.jsx`: OK, 0 warnings.
- All 4 i18n locale files parse and contain every required `comments.*`
  key — 124 checks, 0 missing.
- Backend health: `curl /api/health` -> 200
  `{status:"ok",database:"connected",tableCount:33}`.
- Live route auth gate: `GET /api/comments?entity_type=client&entity_id=119`
  (no auth) -> `{"error":"No token provided"}` (401-equivalent).
- End-to-end smoke test (direct service calls against live `prtop.db`):
  - therapist default create -> visibility=private
  - therapist explicit -> visibility=shared
  - client default create -> visibility=shared
  - client explicit -> visibility=private
  - therapist list returns own private + own shared + client shared, NOT
    client private
  - client list returns therapist shared + own shared + own private, NOT
    therapist private
  - therapist toggle private->shared makes the comment visible to the
    client on next list
  - cross-therapist isolation: a different therapist gets 403 on list
  - non-author patch attempt -> 403
  - delete cleanup OK; therapist_notes -> comments migration count is
    correct (12/12)
- Mock data grep on services/comments.js, routes/comments.js,
  components/CommentsPanel.jsx: zero hits for globalThis|devStore|
  dev-store|mockDb|mockData|fakeData|sampleData|dummyData|testData|MOCK.
- Persistence: all writes flow through `db.run` + `saveDatabaseAfterWrite()`
  to `prtop.db` (sql.js); no in-memory shortcuts.

### Current Status

## Session: 2026-05-05 - Feature #366 (T-08 Custom summary prompts per modality) - PASSING

### Completed: T-08 — Modality-specific AI summary presets + custom prompt

**Why this feature exists:**
Per the alexey_*_2026-04-* interview (p.227-269), a psychoanalyst needs a
fundamentally different session summary than a CBT or NLP practitioner. The
psychodynamic therapist wants transference, defenses, dream material, and
the alliance itself; the CBT therapist wants automatic thoughts, distortions,
behavioral patterns and homework outcomes; the NLP / strategic worker wants
outcome framing, representational systems and ecology checks; the gestalt
therapist wants here-and-now awareness, contact-boundary disturbances and
unfinished business. Without modality-specific framing every therapist gets
the same neutral summary that nobody finds genuinely useful.

T-08 lets each therapist pick one of 5 modality presets in Settings, plus an
optional custom prompt that either appends to (default) or replaces the
preset. Presets live in code (services/ai/summary-presets.js) — NOT in DB —
so they evolve with the product. Custom prompt is Class A encrypted at the
app layer because it can contain therapist working notes / IP.

**State at start of this session:**
The bulk of T-08 had already been built across earlier sessions:
  - `src/backend/src/services/ai/summary-presets.js` — 5 presets
    (psychoanalysis, cbt, nlp, gestalt, generic) with distinct system-prompt
    fragments, `buildModalitySection({specialization, customPrompt,
    customPromptMode})`, `isValidSpecialization`, `listPresets`,
    `CUSTOM_PROMPT_MAX_LENGTH=2000`, `DEFAULT_SPECIALIZATION='generic'`.
  - `src/backend/src/db/connection.js` (lines 1141-1199): idempotent
    migrations adding `users.summary_specialization`,
    `users.custom_summary_prompt_encrypted`,
    `users.custom_summary_prompt_mode` (default 'append'),
    `users.custom_summary_prompt_key_id`,
    `users.custom_summary_prompt_payload_version`. One-shot backfill sets
    every existing therapist + superadmin to 'generic'.
  - `src/backend/src/routes/settings.js`: GET /api/settings/summary +
    PATCH /api/settings/summary. PATCH validates specialization against
    summaryPresets.VALID_SPECIALIZATIONS (400 on bad), enforces 2000-char
    limit on custom_prompt (400 on oversize), validates mode is
    'append'|'replace' (400 otherwise). Empty custom_prompt clears the
    column trio. Non-empty values are encrypted via the standard Class A
    `encrypt()` helper and stored with key_id + payload_version metadata.
    GET decrypts and returns `{summary, presets, max_custom_prompt_length}`.
  - `src/backend/src/services/summarization.js`: `processSessionSummary`
    loads the therapist's specialization + decrypted custom prompt and
    forwards them to `buildSystemPrompt`, which calls
    `summaryPresets.buildModalitySection` and inserts the resulting
    "## Modality Focus" section into the AI system prompt before the client
    context block. Failures during preference load are non-fatal — fallback
    to 'generic'.
  - `src/frontend/src/pages/Settings.jsx`: full Summary Specialization
    section (data-testid="summary-specialization-section") with
    dropdown (`summary-specialization-select`) populated from
    GET /api/settings/summary's `presets` array, live preset description
    text, custom-prompt textarea with character counter and 2000-char cap,
    radio toggle for append-vs-replace mode, save button with success
    toast, fetched on mount via fetchSummarySettings(token).
  - `src/frontend/src/i18n/en.json` + `ru.json`: full
    `settings.summary.*` namespace including title, desc,
    specializationLabel, customPromptLabel/Hint/Placeholder/ModeLabel,
    modeAppend/ReplaceLabel/Hint, save/saved, and presets.<id>.label /
    .description for all 5 modalities.

**What was missing:**
The two remaining locales — `es.json` (Spanish) and `uk.json` (Ukrainian) —
had no `settings.summary` namespace at all. The product spec mandates
EN/RU/ES/UK coverage across every UI string, so without these the Settings
page would render the literal i18n key strings (e.g. "settings.summary.title")
to Spanish- and Ukrainian-speaking therapists.

**What was built this session:**
- `src/frontend/src/i18n/es.json`: added the full `settings.summary` block
  in Spanish (37 lines), including:
    - 13 flat keys (title, desc, specializationLabel,
      customPromptLabel/Hint/Placeholder/ModeLabel, modeAppend/ReplaceLabel
      /Hint, save, saved)
    - Nested `presets.{psychoanalysis,cbt,nlp,gestalt,generic}` each with
      `label` + `description`. Translations use modality-appropriate
      Spanish vocabulary (e.g. "Psicoanálisis / orientado a la profundidad",
      "Terapia Cognitivo-Conductual (TCC)", "PNL / estratégica / breve",
      "Gestalt", "Genérico / integrativo").
- `src/frontend/src/i18n/uk.json`: added the matching block in Ukrainian
  (37 lines), mirroring the Russian translation but with proper Ukrainian
  forms (e.g. "Спеціалізація summary", "Психоаналіз / глибинна робота",
  "Когнітивно-поведінкова терапія (КПТ)", "Гештальт", "Універсальний /
  інтегративний").

Both edits were inserted directly after the existing `settings.reminders`
block so the JSON structure mirrors EN/RU exactly.

**Verification this session:**
- `node -c` clean for the four touched backend files (db/connection.js,
  routes/settings.js, services/summarization.js,
  services/ai/summary-presets.js).
- All 4 i18n JSON files parse cleanly. A 4-locale × (13 flat keys + 5
  preset entries × 2 sub-keys) check (.tmp_check_i18n_summary.js) reported
  0 missing keys.
- esbuild JSX compile (target=es2020, jsx=automatic) of Settings.jsx:
  0 warnings, 0 errors.
- Unit smoke test (.tmp_smoke_summary_presets.js) on the presets module:
    * All 5 presets produce distinct modality sections (verified by
      pairwise inequality check across all C(5,2)=10 pairs).
    * Each section mentions the right modality name (Psychoanalytic, CBT,
      NLP, Gestalt, Generic).
    * Append mode: output contains both the preset's text AND the custom
      prompt under the "### Therapist's additional summarization notes"
      header.
    * Replace mode: output contains the custom prompt but NOT the preset
      text — verified specifically that "Cognitive Triangle" / "SUDS"
      tokens are gone from a CBT replace.
    * Unknown / null specialization falls back to the generic preset.
    * Oversize custom prompt (2000+1500 chars) is clamped to exactly 2000
      chars in the rendered section.
    * `listPresets()` returns 5 entries each with id+description.
- Backend was restarted to pick up the routes/settings.js /summary handler
  (the running instance pre-dated it). Health check post-restart:
  `{status:"ok",database:"connected",tableCount:33}`.
- End-to-end live HTTP test (.tmp_e2e_summary_persistence.js) hitting
  the running backend:
    1. CSRF + login as superadmin succeeded; cookies + token captured.
    2. PATCH /api/settings/summary with
       `{specialization:'cbt', custom_prompt:'RESTART_TEST_<rand>',
        custom_prompt_mode:'replace'}` → 200 with echoed values.
    3. GET /api/settings/summary → 200; returned the same probe value
       (decrypt round-trip works) and the full 5-preset list.
    4. **Backend killed (PID 17536) and re-started (PID 18608); health
       check came back up within ~2s.**
    5. Re-login + GET /api/settings/summary → probe value still present
       (specialization='cbt', custom_prompt='RESTART_TEST_<rand>'). This
       confirms BOTH the plaintext spec column AND the
       custom_summary_prompt_encrypted column survive a full process
       restart — i.e. they persist to prtop.db and are decrypted on
       subsequent reads.
    6. Validation: PATCH with `specialization:'astrology'` → 400.
    7. Validation: PATCH with `custom_prompt='X'.repeat(2001)` → 400.
    8. Cleanup PATCH back to (generic, '', append) → 200.
- Mock data grep on summary-presets.js, routes/settings.js,
  Settings.jsx: zero hits for globalThis|devStore|dev-store|mockDb|

## Session: 2026-05-05 - Feature #360 (T-02 Session date-based ID + calendar) - PASSING

### Completed: T-02 — Sessions identified by meeting_date + calendar widget on client page

**Why this feature exists:**
Per the Misha Drozd interview (docs/new_fichas/customer-development-meetings/
misha_drozd_2026-04-19.md, lines 46-86), a therapist navigating a client's
file should think in dates ("the session on April 15"), not in topic
strings. Sessions are the unit of clinical work, and the calendar metaphor
("точки на датах встреч") is what therapists already know from their
paper diaries. T-02 makes meeting_date the canonical identifier of a
session — distinct from the upload time (created_at) — and surfaces the
calendar widget directly on the client detail page, with click-through to
the session page. T-02 also closes the loop with T-01: every session may
optionally belong to an inquiry, and the calendar/list can be filtered to
a single inquiry thread.

**State at start of this session:**
A large portion of T-02 was already partially built across earlier
sessions for adjacent features (T-01, T-07, T-15):
  - sessions.title and sessions.inquiry_id columns existed (added by T-07)
  - sessions.scheduled_at existed and was being treated as meeting_date
  - POST /api/sessions accepted scheduled_at + title + inquiry_id
  - ClientDetail.jsx already had a metadata form (date / title / inquiry)
    above the dropzone (T-07)

What was missing:
  1. A live calendar widget on the client detail page, with dots on dates
     that have at least one session, click-through to the session.
  2. Inquiry filter on the sessions list (so a therapist working an
     "anxiety" inquiry sees only those sessions).
  3. ORDER BY meeting_date (not created_at) on both the list endpoint and
     the bot endpoint.
  4. PATCH support for meeting_date / title / inquiry_id on
     /api/sessions/:id (only post_session_notes was supported).
  5. /api/bot/sessions/:telegram_id endpoint and the corresponding
     /sessions bot command (the spec requires "last 5 sessions with
     dates").
  6. T-02 specific i18n: session.calendar.* keys in en/ru/es/uk and bot
     translations sessionsHeader/sessionsEmpty/sessionsFailed.

**What was built this session (the gaps above):**

Backend (`src/backend/src/db/connection.js`):
  - T-02 idempotent migration block (lines ~1097-1124):
      * Backfill UPDATE sessions SET scheduled_at = created_at WHERE
        scheduled_at IS NULL OR scheduled_at = '' (only changes rows that
        need it; logs the count when non-zero).
      * CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_sessions_client_meeting
        ON sessions(client_id, scheduled_at) — for the client-page
        calendar query.
      * CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_sessions_therapist_meeting
        ON sessions(therapist_id, scheduled_at) — for the dashboard-wide
        date scans the analytics tab will eventually use.

Backend (`src/backend/src/routes/clients.js` GET /:id/sessions):
  - Added inquiry_id query parameter (positive int, 'none', 'null', or
    omitted). Bad values return 400.
  - Selected columns now include title and inquiry_id, both projected onto
    the JSON response.
  - ORDER BY changed to COALESCE(scheduled_at, created_at) DESC,
    created_at DESC — so the calendar lists in true meeting-date order.
  - Each row exposes both `scheduled_at` (legacy) and `meeting_date` (new
    canonical name) so old callers keep working.

Backend (`src/backend/src/routes/sessions.js` PATCH /:id):
  - Extended supported fields from {post_session_notes} to
    {post_session_notes, title, meeting_date | scheduled_at, inquiry_id}.
  - Each field validated upfront (no half-updates):
      * title: ≤200 chars, null clears
      * meeting_date: YYYY-MM-DD or full ISO 8601, null clears, anything
        else 400
      * inquiry_id: positive int that belongs to the same therapist+client
        pair (cross-therapist / cross-client returns 400). null detaches.
  - Each field updated independently with its own audit_log row
    (session_update_title / session_update_meeting_date /
    session_update_inquiry).
  - Response re-reads the canonical row so the client sees whatever the
    DB actually stored after the write.
  - GET /api/sessions/:id now also returns title + inquiry_id +
    meeting_date alias.

Backend (`src/backend/src/routes/bot.js`):
  - New GET /api/bot/sessions/:telegram_id endpoint behind botAuth.
    Looks up client by telegram_id, returns the last N sessions ordered
    by COALESCE(scheduled_at, created_at) DESC. Each row carries id,
    meeting_date, title, status. Default limit = 5; max clamped to 25.
    No transcript / summary leaks here — Class A material stays in the
    therapist dashboard; the bot is a client-facing surface.
  - 404 if telegram_id has no user, 403 if the user is not a client.

Bot (`src/bot/src/index.js`):
  - Registered /sessions in setMyCommands for clients.
  - New handleSessions(chatId, telegramId, lang) function: calls the API,
    formats meeting_date in the user's timezone using the right locale
    (ru-RU / es-ES / uk-UA / en-US), prints "{i}. 🎧 {date} — {title}
    _(status)_" — title and status omitted when absent.
  - Wired onText(/\/sessions/) to handleSessions.

Frontend (`src/frontend/package.json`):
  - Added "react-day-picker": "^9.14.0" + "date-fns": "^4.1.0" deps.
    Both already installed in node_modules.

Frontend (`src/frontend/src/components/SessionCalendar.jsx`, new file):
  - Reusable calendar component built on top of react-day-picker.
  - Props: sessions, onSelectDate(date, sessionsForDate),
    onUnselectedDateClick(date), locale.
  - Computes a YYYY-MM-DD key per session (handles both 'YYYY-MM-DD'
    and full ISO datetimes; treats naked datetimes as UTC to avoid
    timezone-bucket drift).
  - Renders DayPicker with a `hasSession` modifier — the parent page
    paints the dot via .rdp-prtop-hasSession CSS.
  - Locales mapped to date-fns: enUS / ru / es / uk.
  - Sunday-start for English, Monday-start for everyone else.
  - data-testid="session-calendar" on the wrapper.

Frontend (`src/frontend/src/pages/ClientDetail.jsx`):
  - Imports SessionCalendar.
  - New state: `sessionsInquiryFilter` ('' | 'none' | <id>).
  - sessionMeetingDate now defaults to today (todayStr) instead of '' so
    the upload form is pre-filled per spec ("default = сегодня").
  - fetchSessions() takes an opts override so changing the inquiry filter
    doesn't race against React's stale state.
  - useEffect re-fetches sessions on inquiryFilter change.
  - New three-column section above the dropzone:
      * Calendar panel (lg:col-span-2) with embedded CSS for the green
        dot under .rdp-prtop-hasSession days.
      * Inquiry filter dropdown (data-testid=sessions-inquiry-filter)
        with options: All / No inquiry / each active inquiry.
      * Clear-filter button + total count.
  - Calendar onSelectDate navigates to /sessions/<latest id on that date>.
  - Sessions list now renders meeting_date instead of created_at on the
    right side, shows the title (when present) above the audio/transcript
    flags, and shows an amber 📌 inquiry badge for sessions linked to an
    inquiry (truncated to 24 chars). Each row carries data-testid
    `session-row-<id>` plus data-meeting-date / data-inquiry-id attrs.

i18n (`src/frontend/src/i18n/{en,ru,es,uk}.json`):
  - Added session.calendar block (9 keys each) per locale:
    title, legend, filterByInquiry, allInquiries, noInquiry, clearFilter,
    totalCount, openSession, noSessionOnDate.
  - Locale-appropriate translations:
    en: "Session calendar / Days with sessions / Filter by inquiry / …"
    ru: "Календарь сессий / Дни с сессиями / Фильтр по запросу / …"
    es: "Calendario de sesiones / Días con sesiones / Filtrar por
        consulta / …"
    uk: "Календар сесій / Дні з сесіями / Фільтр за запитом / …"

Bot i18n (`src/bot/src/i18n.js`):

## Session: 2026-05-06 - T-19 Single-track (therapist-only) recording (#377)

Feature #377 PASSING. End-to-end wired: upload form -> diarization ->
speaker selection -> transcription with speaker filter -> summary on
filtered transcript only. Persistence verified across backend restart.
Mixed-mode legacy flow unchanged.

Backend changes:
- routes/sessions.js: POST /api/sessions accepts recording_mode='single_track';
  INSERT saves recording_mode; status starts at 'diarizing' (not 'pending').
  For single_track, async dispatch is processSessionDiarization() instead of
  the transcription chain. GET /api/sessions/:id now returns recording_mode,
  selected_speaker_label, and (only while pending selection) parsed speakers
  array. New POST /api/sessions/:id/select-speaker endpoint validates the
  chosen label, persists selected_speaker_label, NULLs out speaker_segments_json
  (per spec: "Removed tracks ARE NOT saved on disk"), moves status ->
  'transcribing', and async-fires the transcription chain. Idempotent for
  repeat clicks (returns already_selected=true).

- services/diarization.js: added processSessionDiarization(sessionId) —
  orchestrator that reads the session, runs diarizeSessionAudio() on the
  encrypted file, persists speaker_segments_json (totalDurationSec +
  speakers[]), and moves status to 'awaiting_speaker_selection'. On failure
  sets 'diarization_failed'. The dev-mode deterministic 2-speaker split
  (file-size based) was already there from schema-prep work; production
  hooks via DIARIZATION_PROVIDER env (whisperx/pyannote/deepgram).

- services/transcription.js: processSessionTranscription now reads
  recording_mode + selected_speaker_label. When single_track + label is set,
  it runs filterTranscriptToSpeaker(rawTranscript, label) before encryption —
  speaker_0 keeps Therapist: lines, drops Client: lines, and injects a
  "Single-track mode: showing only therapist voice" marker so the filter is
  auditable in the saved transcript. Vector-embedding + summary downstream
  see only the filtered text.

- db/connection.js: T-19 status-constraint migration. The original
  sessions.status CHECK only allowed
  'pending'/'transcribing'/'summarizing'/'complete'/'failed'. Added a one-shot
  rebuild that detects the legacy CHECK in sqlite_master and rebuilds the
  table without it (TEXT, no CHECK), preserving every existing column + row.
  PRAGMA-driven so column list stays in sync. Re-creates the calendar/inquiry/
  therapist_client indexes after rebuild. renderDefault() helper handles
  datetime('now') by re-wrapping function defaults in parens.

Frontend changes:
- pages/ClientDetail.jsx: added sessionSingleTrack state + "Keep only my
  voice (single-track)" checkbox above the dropzone with hint copy.
  handleSessionUpload appends recording_mode='single_track' to formData when
  checked. Reset on successful upload.

- pages/SessionDetail.jsx: new single-track section between the audio player
  and the transcript. Shows "detecting speakers…" while status=diarizing
  (auto-polls every 4s). Shows a speaker picker grid while
  status=awaiting_speaker_selection — each card has a 10-sec preview button
  (fetches the session /stream as a Blob, sets src, seeks to
  preview_start_sec, stops via timeupdate when crossing preview_end_sec) and
  a "This is my voice" button that POSTs /select-speaker. Shows a
  confirmation banner once selected. Failure mode shows diarizationFailed
  copy. New "Single-track" badge in the page header next to the status pill.

i18n:

  label/hint/badge/diarizing/diarizationFailed/awaitingSelection/
  awaitingSelectionHint/speakerLabel/previewWindow/totalSpoken/playPreview/
  stopPreview/selectThisVoice/selecting/selectError/selectedThisVoice/
  transcribingSelected/summaryFromSingleTrack/noPreviewAvailable.

## Session: 2026-05-06 - T-14 Exercise library content cleanup (#372)

Feature #372 PASSING. Marina's interview verdict (misha_drozd_2026-04-19,
lines 410-533) drove three concrete content changes to the seeded
exercise library; all 16 cards audited, 1 removed (Cognitive Reframing
— "слишком общая штука, и она не рабочая"), 2 rewritten with citable
CBT/protocol references, 13 left intact (Habit Tracking is the etalon).
Existing prtop.db rows migrated in place via a new idempotent T-14
cleanup pass in db/connection.js — fresh-DB seed and live-DB migration
now produce identical content.

### Changes

**Backend src/backend/src/routes/exercises.js** (seed function for
fresh DB installs):

1. **Removed "Cognitive Reframing"** seed entry. Marina's reasoning:
   in NLP/CBT "reframing" can refer to 100 different exercises, the
   single card pretending to be "the" reframing exercise looked
   amateurish, and the steps relied on the client inventing their own
   alternative interpretations — therapy work that the client cannot
   do alone between sessions.

2. **Tightened "4-7-8 Breathing"** from 4 -> 6 concrete steps with
   explicit setup (tongue position, posture) + frequency cue
   ("once or twice per day") and Andrew Weil citation in the
   description ("Breathing: The Master Key to Self-Healing").

3. **Rewrote "Evidence Examination"** from 5 vague steps
   ("Evaluate objectively / Formulate a balanced belief") -> 7
   concrete dispute prompts (Beck, "Cognitive Therapy of Depression",
   1979): write the belief in one sentence, rate belief 0-100%, list
   3 supporting + 3 contradicting facts with date+place, "what would
   you tell a friend" prompt, balanced "Sometimes X happens, but Y is
   also true" template, re-rate.

All three rewrites done synchronously in EN/RU/ES/UK.

**Backend src/backend/src/db/connection.js** — new T-14 migration
block (right before the Ukrainian translation backfill):

- Idempotent in-place migration that detects OLD-content signatures and
  applies the new content. Runs on every backend boot but the signature
  checks (LIKE '%Repeat 3-4 cycles%' / LIKE '%Evaluate objectively%')
  fail-fast on already-migrated DBs, so re-runs are no-ops.
- For "Cognitive Reframing": deletes the row only when zero
  exercise_deliveries reference it (FK safety). If deliveries exist, a
  warn-level log line surfaces it for manual triage instead of breaking
  existing assignments.
- Filters all branches by is_custom = 0 so therapist-authored custom
  exercises are never touched.
- Wrapped in a single try/catch with logger.warn fallback so a partial
  schema state (e.g. exercise_deliveries table missing) cannot crash
  the whole boot.

**No frontend changes needed** — T-13's TemplateBadge ("Пример" /
"Template") already labels seeded cards as examples in the library and
detail-modal UI per Marina's "нужно в каждом писать. Пример" feedback,
so the framing concern is already covered.

## Session: 2026-05-06 - T-18 Extended consent disclaimer (#376)

Feature #376 PASSING. The T-18 multi-checkbox consent flow is fully wired
end-to-end: bot disclaimer body + 5 inline checkboxes; client cannot
proceed without ticking all five; clicking *I agree and connect* submits
to /api/bot/consent with version + sha256 hash + mode='connect';
existing clients with stored consent_version < CONSENT_TEXT_VERSION are
re-prompted automatically on their next bot interaction (mode='reconsent'
path). Persistence verified across backend restart.

Bot changes (already in tree from prior commits):
- src/bot/src/index.js: CONSENT_TEXT_VERSION=1 + CONSENT_POINTS array
  ['storage','ai','supervision','revoke','encryption']. pendingConsents
  in-memory state (cleared after submit/cancel). buildConsentBodyText()
  composes the disclaimer header (with therapist display_name + version)
  + the five numbered points + footer. computeConsentHash() returns
  sha256 hex of the rendered body for audit forensics.
  buildConsentKeyboard() renders one row per point (toggling ⬜/✅) +
  Continue + Cancel rows. sendConsentPrompt(chatId, telegramId, lang,
  therapistId, therapistName, mode) sets up state + sends the message;
  re-consent mode prepends a "consent updated, please re-confirm" header
  message before the disclaimer.
  requireConsentUpToDate(chatId, telegramId, lang, user) is the gate
  helper; called from /sos, /diary intake, /exercises, /sessions, /help,
  and other write paths. Returns false + sends the re-consent prompt
  when consent_version < CONSENT_TEXT_VERSION.
  Three callback_data handlers: consent_chk_<tid>_<point> toggles,
  consent_continue_<tid> validates allChecked + posts to backend,
  consent_cancel_<tid> clears state and audits the decline. Backward
  compat: legacy consent_yes_/consent_no_ callbacks still recognised
  (one-message bots from before T-18 still work, version stays at 0).

- src/bot/src/i18n.js: 19 consent.disclaimer.* keys across en/ru/es/uk
  (76 total). Verified all 76 resolve to non-empty strings.

Backend changes (already in tree):
- src/backend/src/routes/bot.js: POST /api/bot/connect now returns
  therapist info + requires_consent=true WITHOUT linking yet; the
  linking step is gated behind /consent. POST /api/bot/consent accepts
  optional consent_version (non-negative integer, defaults 0) +
  consent_text_hash (64-char hex sha256, persisted as null otherwise)
  + mode ('connect' | 'reconsent'). For mode='reconsent' on an
  already-linked client to the SAME therapist, skips the
  client-limit re-check and updates only consent_version +
  consent_text_hash, audit-log action 'consent_reconfirmed'. New helper
  endpoints: GET /api/bot/therapist-display/:id (email/fallback for
  re-consent header) and GET /api/bot/consent-status/:telegram_id (used
  by the bot to read a client's current version on demand).

- src/backend/src/db/connection.js: T-18 idempotent ALTER TABLE migration
  adding users.consent_version (INTEGER DEFAULT 0) +
  users.consent_text_hash (TEXT). Backfills NULL consent_version=0 so
  existing connected clients are correctly version-gated to 0 and will
  be re-prompted by the bot. Verified on backend start: column add
  silently skipped when already present (no log noise on second boot).

## Session: 2026-05-07 - T-20 Auto-link audio by date/metadata (#378)

Feature #378 PASSING. The Sonnet 4.6 path was clear: a tiny, side-effect-
free backend endpoint that returns matching hints, plus a dedicated bulk-
upload page that uses it as a per-file pre-flight before re-using the
existing single-file POST /api/sessions for the real upload (so consent +
plan limit + AES file encryption stay unchanged).

### Why this feature exists

Customer development with Alexey (docs/new_fichas/customer-development-
meetings/alexey_*_2026-04-* p.195-213) surfaced a recurring frustration:
on a busy day a therapist may record 3-5 sessions, then later that
evening drag a folder of files into the dashboard, only to have to set
the client + meeting date for each one by hand. The patterns are
predictable — recorder filenames almost always carry an ISO-ish date,
and even when they don't (Zoom's "Recording 2026-04-19 14_30_00.mp4",
phone recorders' "REC_20260419.m4a", iOS Voice Memos' clean
"untitled.m4a"), the OS-level lastModified mtime is an excellent
fallback. Combined with the calendar slots created by T-02
(sessions.scheduled_at) and T-07 (the "New Session" form with
meeting_date), we have everything we need to auto-suggest a client per
file and let the therapist just say "yes, upload them all".

### Backend

src/backend/src/routes/sessions.js — new POST /api/sessions/auto-match,
authenticated + therapist-only.

Request:
  { files: [{ filename, last_modified_ms? }, ...] }   (max 20 per call)

Response:
  { matches: [{
      file_index, filename,
      parsed_date, parsed_method,
      candidates: [{ client_id, display_name, existing_session_id,
                     existing_session_title, match_reason }],
      auto_match | null,
      conflict, needs_new_session
  }] }

Per-file logic:
  - Parse a date out of the filename (ISO YMD, US MDY, EU DMY) — patterns
    cover Zoom/OBS/dictaphones/macOS/Windows screen recorders. Fail-fast
    on invalid month/day; round-trip through Date.UTC to reject things
    like 2026-02-30.
  - If the filename has nothing recognisable, fall back to the
    File.lastModified mtime; result tagged parsed_method='mtime' so the
    UI can hint that it used a softer signal.
  - Look up the therapist's sessions by DATE(scheduled_at)=parsed_date,
    join against the consenting-client list (consent_therapist_access=1
    AND therapist_id=me) to drop disconnected clients.
  - 1 unique candidate -> auto_match populated.
  - 2+ unique candidates -> conflict=true (UI dropdown).
  - 0 candidates -> needs_new_session=true (UI offers full client picker
    + manual meeting_date, reuses the T-07 path).

The endpoint never touches files on disk and never creates DB rows — it
only returns hints. The actual upload still goes through the existing
POST /api/sessions for each file (already audited, encrypted, plan-
limit-checked, consent-gated). One audit_logs row per call with
action='session_auto_match' for forensics.

Validation hardening:
  - non-array body -> 400
  - empty array -> 200 with []
  - >20 files -> 400 ("Too many files (max 20 per call)")
  - missing/invalid Authorization -> 401
  - non-therapist role -> 403

### Frontend

src/frontend/src/pages/BulkUpload.jsx — new dedicated /sessions/bulk
route, mounted in src/frontend/src/App.jsx behind the existing
GuardedLayout (AuthGuard + TherapistGuard + AppLayout).

UI flow:
  1. Drop zone (drag-and-drop + click-to-browse, multi-file <input>).
     Per-file validation matches the existing single-upload (100MB cap,
     mp3/m4a/wav/mp4/webm/ogg/aac/flac).
  2. On drop, the page POSTs the file metadata to /sessions/auto-match
     and splices the response back into the per-file row state.
  3. Each row renders:
       - filename + size + a status badge
         (Auto-matched / Conflict / No match / Invalid / Uploading /
         Uploaded / Error)
       - parsed-date hint ("Date from filename: 2026-04-19" or "Date
         from file timestamp: ...")
       - <select> with two optgroups: "Same-day sessions" candidates
         first, then "All clients" so the therapist can override.
       - <input type="date"> meeting date (defaulted from parsed_date,
         editable, max=today)
       - <input> session title (optional, 200-char cap)
       - per-file progress bar + Retry button on error
  4. "Upload all ready (N)" button kicks off a sliding-window of
     MAX_PARALLEL_UPLOADS=3 in-flight POST /api/sessions calls. Each
     row's progress bar updates from xhr.upload.onprogress (real
     XMLHttpRequest, same pattern as ClientDetail.jsx).
  5. Status counters at the top (Ready / Conflict / Uploading / Done /
     Errors). Done badge stays so the therapist can see what's already
     persisted.

src/frontend/src/pages/Dashboard.jsx — new card "Bulk session upload"
right above the "Ask About a Client" card, single button -> /sessions/
bulk. data-testid="dashboard-bulk-upload-link" so future regression
tests can spot it.

Pre-loads the consenting-client list once on mount via paginated
GET /api/clients (per_page=100, up to 5 pages — covers any plan tier).
Filters out non-consenting clients before populating dropdowns.

### i18n

session.upload.autoLink.* (37 keys per locale × en/ru/es/uk = 148):
  pageTitle, pageDesc, backToDashboard,
  dragDrop, dropHere, batchHint, tooManyFiles,
  loadingClients, matching, autoMatchError,
  networkError, timeout, empty,
  uploadAll, uploadingAll, clearAll, removeFile, retry,
  clientLabel, clientPick, candidatesGroup, allClientsGroup,
  existingSession,
  parsedFilename, parsedMtime, noDateParsed,
  statusReady, statusConflict, statusUploading, statusDone,
  statusErrored, statusInvalid, statusUploaded, statusError,
  statusAutoMatched, statusConflictBadge, statusNoMatchBadge

dashboard.bulkUpload, dashboard.bulkUploadHint, dashboard.bulkUploadCta
in all four locales for the new dashboard card.

All four locale files validated as parseable JSON post-edit; 37 autoLink
keys present in every locale (verified via _t20_validate_locales.js).

## Session: T-06 Solo mode (Feature #364) — PASSING

### Goal
Allow therapists (psychoanalysts, those working with paranoid clients, or
anyone who simply wants a personal case-file notebook) to create "clients"
that live entirely on the therapist side — no Telegram bot connection, no
invite code, no client-facing flow. Add 'mode' field to existing client
entity (don't create a parallel one).

### Backend (existing prior to this session)

src/backend/src/db/connection.js — users.mode column ('bot_connected' default,
'solo' for therapist-only). Backfill UPDATE on every boot ensures legacy
client rows stay 'bot_connected'.

src/backend/src/routes/clients.js
  - POST /api/clients/solo — creates solo client with:
      mode='solo', telegram_id=NULL, invite_code=NULL,
      consent_therapist_access=1 (auto-granted), consent_version=0.
      Optional initial note encrypted into therapist_notes.
      Plan client-limit enforced; bad email / oversize note rejected 400.
  - GET /api/clients — returns mode in response (default 'bot_connected').
  - GET /api/clients/:id — returns mode.
  - POST /api/clients/:id/exercises — 403 with explanatory error when
    mode='solo' (exercises require a Telegram-connected client).

Bot endpoints under /api/bot/* look up by telegram_id; solo clients have
telegram_id=NULL so any bot-side request for a solo client naturally
404s (defense-in-depth — verified end-to-end).

### Frontend (this session)

src/frontend/src/components/CreateSoloClient.jsx — new modal component:
  - First name / last name / optional email / language / optional initial
    note (≤2000 chars, char counter).
  - Validates locally (need at least one identifier; cap note length).
  - POSTs to /api/clients/solo with bearer + CSRF; on success calls
    onCreated() and closes.
  - Disclaimer panel reminds the therapist that diary/exercises/SOS are
    not available in solo mode.

src/frontend/src/pages/ClientList.jsx
  - Imports CreateSoloClient.
  - Added "📓 Solo Client" button (indigo) next to "Import Clients".
  - SoloBadge component appears next to client name in list rows when
    client.mode === 'solo'.
  - Telegram column shows '—' for solo (was already '—' since
    telegram_id=null, but now styled as indigo to match badge).
  - Empty state ("no clients yet") gets a second action button to create
    a solo client immediately.
  - Switches displayed name to first/last + email/telegram fallback chain.

src/frontend/src/pages/ClientDetail.jsx
  - Solo badge ("📓 Solo") rendered in header next to client name.
  - Header subtitle "Therapist-only notebook · no bot connection" for solo.
  - Tabs Diary, Exercises, and SOS hidden when client.mode === 'solo'.
  - useEffect snaps activeTab back to 'timeline' if a solo client lands on
    a hidden tab via stale URL / back button.
  - All tabs gated on isSolo as a single (() => { ... return <div>...</div>; })()
    wrapper so the tab-bar JSX stays a single React element.

### i18n

Added client.mode.{solo,botConnected,soloDash} and client.solo.{title,
badge,badgeTooltip,description,subtitle,btn,btnTooltip,firstName,lastName,
emailOptional,language,noteOptional,notePlaceholder,disclaimer,creating,
